! Title: Mork's Filter List
! Description: This list contains domains that I deemed unsafe or untrusted formatted into host file format. If you found a website here that you think should not be blocked don't bother, I won't remove it unless I choose to do so. I create this block list for personal purposes go create your own if you want.
! Author: MORK
! Author Contact: https://discord.com/users/1070905639162875905
! Homepage: https://github.com/HiImMork/block-list
! URL: https://github.com/HiImMork/block-list/blob/main/Mork's%20Filter%20List.txt
